# Tedim Chin: Entries Requiring Review

These entries were excluded from the polished sample dictionary because
they have unresolved gloss ambiguity, mixed lexical/grammatical status,
or other issues requiring human review.

**Total entries:** 269

## Review Categories

- Mixed lexical/grammatical: 21
- Polysemous (needs sense separation): 66
- Unsafe gloss: 0
- Grammatical words needing review: 0
- Affixes needing review: 169
- Other: 13

### hi

**Citation form:** hi
**POS:** V
**Entry status:** clean
**Frequency:** 55024 tokens
**Tentative primary:** DECL
**Corpus distribution:** DECL:47708, this:6100, be:620, 3SG:283, 1PL.INCL:206
**Flags:** polysemous, primarily_grammatical, needs_review
**Notes:** sentence-final declarative marker (88% of uses)

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01001001] A kipat cil-in Pasian in vantung le leitung a piangsak hi.
   *hi* / DECL
   — In the beginning God created the heaven and the earth.
2. [01001003] Pasian in, “Khuavak om hen,” ci hi; tua ciangin khuavak om pah hi.
   *hi* / DECL
   — And God said, Let there be light: and there was light.
3. [01001002] Leitung in limlemel nei loin a awngthawlpi ahi hi. Tuipi tung tengah khua mial bikbek a, tua tui tungah Pasian' Kha in na a sem hi.
   *hi* / DECL
   — And the earth was without form, and void; and darkness was upon the face of the deep. And the Spirit of God moved upon the face of the waters.
4. [01001004] Pasian in tua khuavak hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi. Pasian in khuamial panin khuavak khenkhia hi.
   *hi* / DECL
   — And God saw the light, that it was good: and God divided the light from the darkness.
5. [01001005] Pasian in khuavak pen “Sun” ci a, khuamial pen “Zan” ci hi. Nitak hong bei-in, zingsang hong tung a, ni khat ni ahi hi.
   *hi* / DECL
   — And God called the light Day, and the darkness he called Night. And the evening and the morning were the first day.

### ding

**Citation form:** ding
**POS:** V
**Entry status:** clean
**Frequency:** 25223 tokens
**Tentative primary:** IRR
**Corpus distribution:** IRR:24295, 2SG:683, stand:228, 3SG:13, REFL:4
**Flags:** polysemous, primarily_grammatical, needs_review
**Notes:** irrealis/prospective marker

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01002015] Topa Pasian in mipa la-in, Eden huan kho-in a kem dingin a koih hi.
   *ding-in* / IRR-ERG
   — And the LORD God took the man, and put him into the garden of Eden to dress it and to keep it.
2. [01002016] Topa Pasian in mipa thu pia a, “Na ut utin huan sung singkung gah khempeuh na ne thei ding hi.
   *ding* / IRR
   — And the LORD God commanded the man, saying, Of every tree of the garden thou mayest freely eat:
3. [01001014] Pasian in, “Sun le zan a khen dingin vantungah khuavakte om hen; tuate pen pawi hun le khuahun, ni le kumte khen nading hi hen la,
   *ding-in* / IRR-ERG
   — And God said, Let there be lights in the firmament of the heaven to divide the day from the night; and let them be for signs, and for seasons, and for days, and years:
4. [01001015] leitung khua a vaksak dingin vantungah khuavak hi uh hen,” ci hi. Tua mah bangin a piang pah hi.
   *ding-in* / IRR-ERG
   — and let them be for lights in the firmament of the heaven to give light upon the earth: and it was so.
5. [01001016] Pasian in khuavak lian nih bawl a, khuavak lianzaw pen sun a uk ding, khuavak neuzaw pen zan a uk dingin bawl a, amah in aksite zong a bawl hi. Leitungah khua a vaksak ding, sun le zan a uk ding, khuamial panin khuavak a khenkhia dingin Pasian in vantungah tuate a koih hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
   *ding* / IRR
   — And God made two great lights; the greater light to rule the day, and the lesser light to rule the night: he made the stars also.

   *hong* / 3→1

   *hong* / 3→1

5. [01001023] Nitak hong bei-in zingsang hong tung a, a ni nga ni ahi hi.
   *hong* / 3→1

### thu

**Citation form:** thu
**POS:** N
**Entry status:** clean
**Frequency:** 10771 tokens
**Tentative primary:** word
**Corpus distribution:** word:9736, law:564, speech:384, knowledge:25, REFL:25
**Flags:** primarily_grammatical
**Notes:** word/matter (not portion)

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01009026] Topa ka Pasian in Shem thupha pia hen la, Kanaan, ama sila hisak hen.
   *thu-pha* / word-good
   — And he said, Blessed be the LORD God of Shem; And Canaan shall be his servant.
2. [01006006] Leitungah mihing a bawl pen Topa khial kisa a, tua thu in ama lungsim dahsak hi.
   *thu* / word
   — And it repented the LORD that he had made man on the earth, and it grieved him at his heart.
3. [01001022] Pasian in amaute thupha pia a, “Ci pha-in tampi pha-in, tuipi sung dim unla, leitungah vasate tampi pha un,” ci hi.
   *thu-pha* / word-good
   — And God blessed them, saying, Be fruitful, and multiply, and fill the waters in the seas, and let fowl multiply in the earth.
4. [01001028] Pasian in amaute thupha pia a, Pasian in amaute tungah, “Ci pha-in tampi pha unla, leitung dimin zo un. Tuipi ngasate tung, leitungah a gamtang, a nungtate khempeuh tungah ukna nei ta un,” a ci hi.
   *thu-pha* / word-good
   — And God blessed them, and God said unto them, Be fruitful, and multiply, and replenish the earth, and subdue it: and have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over every living thing that moveth upon the earth.
5. [01002003] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ni sagih ni thupha pia-in siangthosak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh piansak nasepna ama nasep khempeuh panin tua ni-in Pasian a tawlnga hi.
   *thu-pha* / word-good
   — And God blessed the seventh day, and sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.

### ciang

**Citation form:** ciang
**POS:** UNK
**Entry status:** clean
**Frequency:** 10644 tokens
**Tentative primary:** then
**Corpus distribution:** then:10590, REFL:20, measure:8, clear:7, weave:5
**Flags:** primarily_grammatical, needs_review

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01001003] Pasian in, “Khuavak om hen,” ci hi; tua ciangin khuavak om pah hi.
   *ciang-in* / then-ERG
   — And God said, Let there be light: and there was light.
2. [01002001] Tua ahih ciangin vantung, leitung, le a sunga omte khempeuh kiman khin hi.
   *ciang-in* / then-ERG
   — Thus the heavens and the earth were finished, and all the host of them.
3. [01001021] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in tuipi ganhing golpite le amau nam ciatin tuipi sungah tampi a pha, nuntakna a nei a gamtang thei ganhing namkim le kha a nei vasa khempeuh amau nam ciatin a piangsak hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
   *ciang-in* / then-ERG
   — And God created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and God saw that it was good.
4. [01001026] Tua ciangin Pasian in, “Eima lim, eimah hong sunin mihing bawl ni. Tuipi ngasate tung, huihlak vasate tung, ganhingte tung, le leitung a a bokvakte khempeuh tungah ukna neisak ni,” a ci hi.
   *ciang-in* / then-ERG
   — And God said, Let us make man in our image, after our likeness: and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea, and over the fowl of the air, and over the cattle, and over all the earth, and over every creeping thing that creepeth upon the earth.
5. [01001027] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ama lim bangin mihing piangsakin, Pasian' lim bangin amah a piangsak hi. Amah in pasal le numei a piangsak hi.
   *ciang-in* / then-ERG
   — So God created man in his own image, in the image of God created he him; male and female created he them.

3. [01001021] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in tuipi ganhing golpite le amau nam ciatin tuipi sungah tampi a pha, nuntakna a nei a gamtang thei ganhing namkim le kha a nei vasa khempeuh amau nam ciatin a piangsak hi. Pasian in tua pen hoih hi, ci-in a mu hi.
   *thei* / know
   — And God created great whales, and every living creature that moveth, which the waters brought forth abundantly, after their kind, and every winged fowl after his kind: and God saw that it was good.
4. [01002009] A deihhuai, nek dinga a hoih singkung nam khempeuh, huan laizangah nuntakna singkung, le a pha le a sia theihna singkung, lei sung panin Topa Pasian in posak hi.

   *kang-tum* / burn-all
   — And it came to pass, when they had brought them forth abroad, that he said, Escape for thy life; look not behind thee, neither stay thou in all the plain; escape to the mountain, lest thou be consumed.

   — save only that which the young men have eaten, and the portion of the men which went with me, Aner, Eshcol, and Mamre; let them take their portion.

   — And they warred against the Midianites, as the LORD commanded Moses; and they slew all the males.
2. [05002032] Tua ciangin Sihon le a mite khempeuh eite a do dingin Jahaz-ah hong pai uh hi.
   *do* / rise
   — Then Sihon came out against us, he and all his people, to fight at Jahaz.
3. [01014015] Amah in zan hunin ama pawlte, amah le a nasemte, amaute a do dingin khenin amaute zo a, Damaskas leilu lam Hobah ciang dong a delh uh hi.
   *do* / rise
   — And he divided himself against them, he and his servants, by night, and smote them, and pursued them unto Hobah, which is on the left hand of Damascus.
4. [02001010] Amaute hong tam kha ding uh ahih manin ngaihsut siamna tawh amaute hih ni. Eite tungah gal hong om leh amaute in i galte pawlin eite hong do-in hih gam panin taikhia kha ding uh hi,” a ci hi.
   *do-in* / rise-ERG
   — come on, let us deal wisely with them; lest they multiply, and it come to pass, that, when there falleth out any war, they join also unto our enemies, and fight against us, and so get them up out of the land.
5. [02013018] Ahih hangin Pasian in San Tuipi lam manawhin sehnel gam lamah mite kot paipih hi. Israel mite gal a do dingin a kithawisa-in Egypt leitang panin a paito uh ahi hi.
   *do* / rise
   — but God led the people about, through the way of the wilderness of the Red sea: and the children of Israel went up harnessed out of the land of Egypt.

   *hial* / EMPH
   — Mine age is departed, and is removed from me as a shepherd's tent: I have cut off like a weaver my life: he will cut me off with pining sickness: From day even to night wilt thou make an end of me.

   — And they said, We cannot, until all the flocks be gathered together, and till they roll the stone from the well's mouth; then we water the sheep.

   *vui* / dust
   — And Sarah died in Kirjath-arba; the same is Hebron in the land of Canaan: and Abraham came to mourn for Sarah, and to weep for her.
4. [01023004] “Kei pen note lakah khualmi hi-in peemta ka hi hi. Ka zi ka vui theih nadingin note' lakah vui nading mun leitang hong pia un,” a ci hi.
   *vui* / dust
   — I am a stranger and a sojourner with you: give me a possession of a buryingplace with you, that I may bury my dead out of my sight.
5. [01023006] “Topa aw, kote' thu hong ngai in. Nang pen kote' lakah a vanglian ulian khat na hi hi. Kote' han na deih pen munah na zi vui in. Kote kuamah in nang a dingin a han it lo ding a, na zi vui ding hong khaktan lo ding hi,” a ci uh hi.
   *vui* / dust
   — Hear us, my lord: thou art a mighty prince among us: in the choice of our sepulchres bury thy dead; none of us shall withhold from thee his sepulchre, but that thou mayest bury thy dead.

### kiat

**Citation form:** kiat
**POS:** AFFIX (inflection)
**Entry status:** affix_review_needed
**Frequency:** 1 tokens
**Tentative primary:** APPL

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01017024] Ama vun dawn a ki-atin Abraham kum sawmkua le kua pha ta hi.
   *kiat-in* / release-ERG
   — And Abraham was ninety years old and nine, when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.
2. [01017026] Tua ni mahmahin Abraham le a tapa Ishmael a vun uh ki-at hi.
   *kiat* / fall
   — In the selfsame day was Abraham circumcised, and Ishmael his son.
3. [01017010] Hih pen nang le nang' khit cianga na suanlekhakte' zuih ding keima thuciamna ahi hi: Note' lak panin pasal peuhmah a vun ki-at ding hi.
   *kiat* / fall
   — This is my covenant, which ye shall keep, between me and you and thy seed after thee; Every man child among you shall be circumcised.
4. [01017011] Note' vun dawn ki-at ding a, tua pen kei le note' kikalah thuciamna lim khat hi ding hi.
   *kiat* / fall
   — And ye shall circumcise the flesh of your foreskin; and it shall be a token of the covenant betwixt me and you.
5. [01017012] Note' lak panin ni giat a pha peuhmah pa a vun ki-at ding hi. Note' khang tawntungin pasal peuhmah, note' inn sunga suak hitaleh, note' ta ahi lo, gamdang mi khatpeuh kiang panin na sum uh tawh na lei uh hitaleh
   *kiat* / fall
   — And he that is eight days old shall be circumcised among you, every man child in your generations, he that is born in the house, or bought with money of any stranger, which is not of thy seed.

### neihkhem

**Citation form:** neihkhem
**POS:** AFFIX (inflection)
**Entry status:** affix_review_needed
**Frequency:** 1 tokens
**Tentative primary:** ERG

**Examples (for review):**
1. [40024011] Kamsang kineihkhem mi tampi hong piang ding a, mi tampi tak umkhialsak ding uh hi.
   *ki-neihkhem* / possess.all
   — And many false prophets shall rise, and shall deceive many.
2. [40015007] Na tungthamun mihoih a kineihkhem mite aw, Isaiah in note' thu a genna man mahmah hi. Tua a genna-ah,
   *ki-neihkhem* / possess.all
   — Ye hypocrites, well did Esaias prophesy of you, saying,
3. [24003010] Hih bang teng hinapi a sanggamnu, numei ginalo Judah, a lungsim takpi tawh hong kilehkik loin, a kilehkik hong kineihkhem bek hi, Topa in kong ci hi,” hong ci hi.
   *ki-neihkhem* / possess.all
   — And yet for all this her treacherous sister Judah hath not turned unto me with her whole heart, but feignedly, saith the LORD .
4. [40006002] “Tua ahih manin mi cimawhte tungah huhna na piak uh ciangin, mite in a phat ding uh a deihna tawh a kineihkhem mite in kikhopna innsung le kongzing lakah a kilang theithei-in a hih uh bangin na hih kei un. Tua bangin a hih mite in thaman a ngah khinta ahihna thu limtakin na phawk un.
   *ki-neihkhem* / possess.all
   — Therefore when thou doest thine alms, do not sound a trumpet before thee, as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets, that they may have glory of men. Verily I say unto you, They have their reward.
5. [40006005] “Note in thu na nget uh ciangin mite' muh theih dingin a kineihkhem mite in kikhopna innsung le kongzing lamka lai-ah a ngetnop se uh bangin na gamta kei un. Tua bangin a gamtate in thaman a ngah khinta ahihna uh limtakin phawk un.
   *ki-neihkhem* / possess.all
   — And when thou prayest, thou shalt not be as the hypocrites are : for they love to pray standing in the synagogues and in the corners of the streets, that they may be seen of men. Verily I say unto you, They have their reward.

### ama

**Citation form:** ama
**POS:** AFFIX (inflection)
**Entry status:** affix_review_needed
**Frequency:** 1 tokens
**Tentative primary:** 3PL

**Examples (for review):**
1. [01008006] Ni sawmli a cin ni ciangin Noah in ama bawlsa teembaw tawlet hong a,
   *ama* / 3SG.POSS
   — And it came to pass at the end of forty days, that Noah opened the window of the ark which he had made:
2. [01006006] Leitungah mihing a bawl pen Topa khial kisa a, tua thu in ama lungsim dahsak hi.
   *ama* / 3SG.POSS
   — And it repented the LORD that he had made man on the earth, and it grieved him at his heart.
3. [01001027] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ama lim bangin mihing piangsakin, Pasian' lim bangin amah a piangsak hi. Amah in pasal le numei a piangsak hi.
   *ama* / 3SG.POSS
   — So God created man in his own image, in the image of God created he him; male and female created he them.
4. [01002002] Ni sagih ma-in Pasian in a nasepte zo khinta a, ama hihsa nasep khempeuh panin ni sagih ni-in a tawlnga hi.
   *ama* / 3SG.POSS
   — And on the seventh day God ended his work which he had made; and he rested on the seventh day from all his work which he had made.
5. [01002003] Tua ahih ciangin Pasian in ni sagih ni thupha pia-in siangthosak hi. Bang hang hiam cih leh piansak nasepna ama nasep khempeuh panin tua ni-in Pasian a tawlnga hi.
   *ama* / 3SG.POSS
   — And God blessed the seventh day, and sanctified it: because that in it he had rested from all his work which God created and made.
